The FINAL PROOF IS AS FOLLOWS
theorem P3 {a b c : ℝ} (ha : a > 0) (hb : b > 0) (hc : c > 0) (h : a * b * c = 1) : 3 / 2 ≤ 1 / (c ^ 3 * (a + b)) + 1 / (a ^ 3 * (b + c)) + 1 / (b ^ 3 * (c + a)) := by  
  make_homogeneous 3 / 2 - ((a * b * c) ^ (4 / 3) / ((a + b) * (c ^ 3))) - ((a * b * c) ^ (4 / 3) / ((a + c) * (b ^ 3))) - ((a * b * c) ^ (4 / 3) / ((a ^ 3) * (b + c))) ≤ 0
  smt_decide!
